    def _handle_tdengine_merge(
        self, data: pd.DataFrame, table_name: str, classification: DataClassification
    ) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """TDengine"""
        # 
        return self._handle_tdengine_latest_wins(data, table_name, classification)

    def _handle_tdengine_reject(
        self, data: pd.DataFrame, table_name: str, classification: DataClassification
    ) -> Optional[pd.DataFrame]:
        """TDengine"""
        try:
            # 
            time_column = "ts" if "ts" in data.columns else "timestamp"
            if time_column not in data.columns:
                return data

            # 
            if "symbol" in data.columns:
                duplicates = data.duplicated(subset=[time_column, "symbol"])
            else:
                duplicates = data.duplicated(subset=[time_column])

            if duplicates.any():
                dup_count = duplicates.sum()
                logger.warning(
                    f"TDengine REJECT {dup_count} "
                )
                return pd.DataFrame()  # DataFrame

            # 
            return data

        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"TDengine REJECT: {e}")
            return data

    def _preprocess_timeseries_data(
        self, data: pd.DataFrame, classification: DataClassification
    ) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """"""
        processed_data = normalize_dataframe(data)

        # 
        if (
            "timestamp" not in processed_data.columns
            and "ts" not in processed_data.columns
        ):
            processed_data["ts"] = datetime.now()
        elif "timestamp" in processed_data.columns:
            processed_data["ts"] = pd.to_datetime(processed_data["timestamp"])
            processed_data.drop("timestamp", axis=1, inplace=True)

        # 
        if classification == DataClassification.TICK_DATA:
            required_columns = ["ts", "symbol", "price", "volume"]
        elif classification == DataClassification.MINUTE_KLINE:
            required_columns = [
                "ts",
                "symbol",
                "open",
                "high",
                "low",
                "close",
                "volume",
            ]
        else:
            required_columns = ["ts", "symbol"]

        # 
        missing_columns = [
            col for col in required_columns if col not in processed_data.columns
        ]
        if missing_columns:
            logger.warning(f": {missing_columns}")

        return processed_data

    def _postprocess_timeseries_data(
        self, data: pd.DataFrame, classification: DataClassification
    ) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """"""
        if data.empty:
            return data

        #

            data = data.sort_values("ts")

        return data

    def _insert_tick_data(self, cursor, data: pd.DataFrame, table_name: str) -> bool:
        """Tick"""
        try:
            # Tick
            insert_sql = f"""
                INSERT INTO {table_name} (ts, symbol, price, volume, amount, exchange)
                VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
            """

            # 
            records = []
            for _, row in data.iterrows():
                records.append(
                    (
                        row.get("ts", datetime.now()),
                        row.get("symbol", ""),
                        row.get("price", 0.0),
                        row.get("volume", 0),
                        row.get("amount", 0.0),
                        row.get("exchange", "SH"),
                    )
                )

            # 
            cursor.executemany(insert_sql, records)
            return True

        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Tick: {e}")
            return False

    def _insert_generic_timeseries(
        self, cursor, data: pd.DataFrame, table_name: str
    ) -> bool:
        """"""
        try:
            # 
            columns = list(data.columns)
            placeholders = ", ".join(["?" for _ in columns])
            insert_sql = f"INSERT INTO {table_name} ({', '.join(columns)}) VALUES ({placeholders})"

            # 
            records = data.values.tolist()

            # 
            cursor.executemany(insert_sql, records)
            return True

        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f": {e}")
            return False

    def _build_timeseries_query(
        self,
        classification: DataClassification,
        table_name: str,
        filters: Dict = None,
        **kwargs,
    ) -> str:
        """"""
        base_query = f"SELECT * FROM {table_name}"

        conditions = []

        # 
        if filters:
            for key, value in filters.items():
                if key == "symbol":
                    if isinstance(value, list):
                        symbols = "','".join(value)
                        conditions.append(f"symbol IN ('{symbols}')")
                    else:
                        conditions.append(f"symbol = '{value}'")
                elif key == "start_time":
                    conditions.append(f"ts >= '{value}'")
                elif key == "end_time":
                    conditions.append(f"ts <= '{value}'")
                elif key == "date_range":
                    if isinstance(value, dict) and "start" in value and "end" in value:
                        conditions.append(
                            f"ts >= '{value['start']}' AND ts <= '{value['end']}'"
                        )

        # kwargs
        if "start_time" in kwargs:
            conditions.append(f"ts >= '{kwargs['start_time']}'")
        if "end_time" in kwargs:
            conditions.append(f"ts <= '{kwargs['end_time']}'")
        if "symbol" in kwargs:
            conditions.append(f"symbol = '{kwargs['symbol']}'")

        # 
        if conditions:
            base_query += " WHERE " + " AND ".join(conditions)

        # 
        base_query += " ORDER BY ts DESC"

        # 
        if "limit" in kwargs:
            base_query += f" LIMIT {kwargs['limit']}"

        return base_query (duplicate-code)

    def _get_postgresql_engine(self, database_name: str):
        """PostgreSQL SQLAlchemy"""
        import sqlalchemy

        # PostgreSQL
        host = os.getenv("POSTGRESQL_HOST")
        user = os.getenv("POSTGRESQL_USER")
        password = os.getenv("POSTGRESQL_PASSWORD")
        port = os.getenv("POSTGRESQL_PORT", "5432")

        # 
        connection_url = (
            f"postgresql+psycopg2://{user}:{password}@{host}:{port}/{database_name}"
        )

        # SQLAlchemy
        engine = sqlalchemy.create_engine(connection_url)
        return engine

    def _upsert_data_with_engine(
        self,
        data: pd.DataFrame,
        table_name: str,
        engine,
        classification: DataClassification,
    ):
        """SQLAlchemyUPSERT"""
        try:
            # UPSERT
            with engine.begin() as conn:
                raw_conn = conn.connection
                affected_rows = self._upsert_data(
                    data, table_name, raw_conn, classification
                )
                logger.info(f"UPSERT: {table_name}, : {affected_rows}")

        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"UPSERT: {e}")
            # 
            try:
                data.to_sql(
                    table_name, engine, if_exists="append", index=False, method="multi"
                )
            except Exception as fallback_error:
                if (
                    "duplicate key" in str(fallback_error).lower()
                    or "unique constraint" in str(fallback_error).lower()
                ):
                    logger.warning(f": {fallback_error}")
                    # UPSERT
                    pass
                else:
                    raise fallback_error

    def _postprocess_analytical_data(
        self, data: pd.DataFrame, classification: DataClassification
    ) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """"""
        if data.empty:
            return data

        # 
        date_columns = ["trade_date", "calc_date", "created_at", "updated_at"]
        for col in date_columns:
            if col in data.columns:
                data[col] = pd.to_datetime(data[col])

        return data

    def _upsert_data(
        self,
        data: pd.DataFrame,
        table_name: str,
        conn,
        classification: DataClassification,
    ):
        """PostgreSQL Upsert - ON CONFLICT"""
        try:
            key_columns = self._get_default_key_columns(classification)
            cursor = conn.cursor()

            # 
            columns = list(data.columns)
            placeholders = ", ".join(["%s"] * len(columns))
            column_names = ", ".join(columns)

            # ON CONFLICT
            conflict_columns = ", ".join(key_columns)

            # UPDATE SET
            update_columns = [col for col in columns if col not in key_columns]
            update_set = ", ".join(
                [f"{col} = EXCLUDED.{col}" for col in update_columns]
            )

            # UPSERT SQL
            upsert_sql = f"""
            INSERT INTO {table_name} ({column_names})
            VALUES ({placeholders})
            ON CONFLICT ({conflict_columns})
            DO UPDATE SET
                {update_set},
                updated_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
            """

            # UPSERT
            records_to_insert = []
            for _, row in data.iterrows():
                record = []
                for col in columns:
                    value = row[col]
                    # NaNpandas
                    if pd.isna(value):
                        record.append(None)
                    elif isinstance(value, pd.Timestamp):
                        record.append(value.to_pydatetime())
                    else:
                        record.append(value)
                records_to_insert.append(tuple(record))

            # UPSERT
            cursor.executemany(upsert_sql, records_to_insert)
            conn.commit()

            logger.info(
                f"PostgreSQL UPSERT: {table_name}, : {len(records_to_insert)}"
            )
            return len(records_to_insert)

        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"PostgreSQL UPSERT: {table_name}, : {e}")
            conn.rollback()
            raise

    def _execute_update(
        self, cursor, data: pd.DataFrame, table_name: str, key_columns: List[str]
    ) -> bool:
        """"""
        try:
            for _, row in data.iterrows():
                # SET
                set_clauses = []
                set_values = []
                for col in data.columns:
                    if col not in key_columns:
                        set_clauses.append(f"{col} = %s")
                        set_values.append(row[col])

                # WHERE
                where_clauses = []
                where_values = []
                for col in key_columns:
                    where_clauses.append(f"{col} = %s")
                    where_values.append(row[col])

                # SQL
                update_sql = f"""
                    UPDATE {table_name}
                    SET {', '.join(set_clauses)}
                    WHERE {' AND '.join(where_clauses)} (duplicate-code)

            data["ts"] = pd.to_datetime(data["ts"])
            data = data.sort_values("ts")

        return data

    def _insert_tick_data(self, cursor, data: pd.DataFrame, table_name: str) -> bool:
        """Tick"""
        try:
            # Tick
            insert_sql = f"""
                INSERT INTO {table_name} (ts, symbol, price, volume, amount, exchange)
                VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
            """

            # 
            records = []
            for _, row in data.iterrows():
                records.append(
                    (
                        row.get("ts", datetime.now()),
                        row.get("symbol", ""),
                        row.get("price", 0.0),
                        row.get("volume", 0),
                        row.get("amount", 0.0),
                        row.get("exchange", "SH"),
                    )
                )

            # 
            cursor.executemany(insert_sql, records)
            return True

        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Tick: {e}")
            return False

    def _insert_minute_kline(self, cursor, data: pd.DataFrame, table_name: str) -> bool:
        """K"""
        try:
            # K
            insert_sql = f"""
                INSERT INTO {table_name} (ts, symbol, open, high, low, close, volume, amount, frequency)
                VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
            """

            #

    def _insert_generic_timeseries(
        self, cursor, data: pd.DataFrame, table_name: str
    ) -> bool:
        """"""
        try:
            # 
            columns = list(data.columns)
            placeholders = ", ".join(["?" for _ in columns])
            insert_sql = f"INSERT INTO {table_name} ({', '.join(columns)}) VALUES ({placeholders})"

            # 
            records = data.values.tolist()

            # 
            cursor.executemany(insert_sql, records)
            return True

        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f": {e}")
            return False

    def _build_timeseries_query(
        self,
        classification: DataClassification,
        table_name: str,
        filters: Dict = None,
        **kwargs,
    ) -> str:
        """"""
        base_query = f"SELECT * FROM {table_name}"

        conditions = []

        # 
        if filters:
            for key, value in filters.items():
                if key == "symbol":
                    if isinstance(value, list):
                        symbols = "','".join(value)
                        conditions.append(f"symbol IN ('{symbols}')")
                    else:
                        conditions.append(f"symbol = '{value}'")
                elif key == "start_time":
                    conditions.append(f"ts >= '{value}'")
                elif key == "end_time":
                    conditions.append(f"ts <= '{value}'")
                elif key == "date_range":
                    if isinstance(value, dict) and "start" in value and "end" in value:
                        conditions.append(
                            f"ts >= '{value['start']}' AND ts <= '{value['end']}'"
                        )

        # kwargs
        if "start_time" in kwargs:
            conditions.append(f"ts >= '{kwargs['start_time']}'")
        if "end_time" in kwargs:
            conditions.append(f"ts <= '{kwargs['end_time']}'")
        if "symbol" in kwargs:
            conditions.append(f"symbol = '{kwargs['symbol']}'")

        # 
        if conditions:
            base_query += " WHERE " + " AND ".join(conditions)

        # 
        base_query += " ORDER BY ts DESC"

        # 
        if "limit" in kwargs:
            base_query += f" LIMIT {kwargs['limit']}"

        return base_query (duplicate-code)

    def _get_default_table_name(self, classification: DataClassification) -> str:
        """"""

            DataClassification.TICK_DATA: "tick_data",

    def _apply_tdengine_deduplication(
        self,
        data: pd.DataFrame,
        table_name: str,
        strategy,
        classification: DataClassification,
    ) -> Optional[pd.DataFrame]:
        """
        TDengine

        Args:
            data: 
            table_name: 
            strategy: 
            classification: 

        Returns:
            
        """
        try:
            from src.core import DeduplicationStrategy

            if strategy == DeduplicationStrategy.LATEST_WINS:
                return self._handle_tdengine_latest_wins(
                    data, table_name, classification
                )
            elif strategy == DeduplicationStrategy.FIRST_WINS:
                return self._handle_tdengine_first_wins(
                    data, table_name, classification
                )
            elif strategy == DeduplicationStrategy.MERGE:
                return self._handle_tdengine_merge(data, table_name, classification)
            elif strategy == DeduplicationStrategy.REJECT:
                return self._handle_tdengine_reject(data, table_name, classification)
            else:
                logger.warning(f"TDengine: {strategy}, ")
                return data

        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"TDengine: {strategy}, : {e}")
            return data

    def _handle_tdengine_latest_wins(
        self, data: pd.DataFrame, table_name: str, classification: DataClassification
    ) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """TDengine"""
        try:
            # symbol
            time_column = "ts" if "ts" in data.columns else "timestamp"
            if time_column not in data.columns:
                logger.warning("")
                return data

            # datetime
            data[time_column] = pd.to_datetime(data[time_column])

            # symbol
            if "symbol" in data.columns:
                deduped_data = data.sort_values([time_column]).drop_duplicates(
                    subset=["symbol", time_column], keep="last"
                )
            else:
                deduped_data = data.sort_values([time_column]).drop_duplicates(
                    subset=[time_column], keep="last"
                )

            removed_count = len(data) - len(deduped_data)
            if removed_count > 0:
                logger.info(
                    f"TDengine LATEST_WINS {removed_count} "
                )

            return deduped_data

        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"TDengine LATEST_WINS: {e}")
            return data

            time_column = "ts" if "ts" in data.columns else "timestamp"

            conn = self.db_manager.get_connection(self.db_type, database_name)

            # 
            min_time = data[time_column].min()
            max_time = data[time_column].max()

            if "symbol" in data.columns:
                symbols = data["symbol"].unique()
                symbols_str = "','".join(symbols)
                query = f"""
                SELECT DISTINCT {time_column}, symbol
                FROM {table_name}
                WHERE {time_column} BETWEEN '{min_time}' AND '{max_time}'
                AND symbol IN ('{symbols_str}')
                """
            else:
                query = f"""
                SELECT DISTINCT {time_column}
                FROM {table_name}
                WHERE {time_column} BETWEEN '{min_time}' AND '{max_time}'
                """

            existing_data = pd.read_sql(query, conn)

            if existing_data.empty:
                return data

            # 
            if "symbol" in data.columns:
                merge_columns = [time_column, "symbol"]
            else:
                merge_columns = [time_column]

            filtered_data = data.merge(
                existing_data, on=merge_columns, how="left", indicator=True
            )
            new_data = filtered_data[filtered_data["_merge"] == "left_only"].drop(
                "_merge", axis=1
            )

            removed_count = len(data) - len(new_data)
            if removed_count > 0:
                logger.info(
                    f"TDengine FIRST_WINS {removed_count} "
                )

            return new_data

        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"TDengine FIRST_WINS: {e}")
            return data

    def _handle_tdengine_merge(
        self, data: pd.DataFrame, table_name: str, classification: DataClassification
    ) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """TDengine"""
        # 
        return self._handle_tdengine_latest_wins(data, table_name, classification)

    def _handle_tdengine_reject(
        self, data: pd.DataFrame, table_name: str, classification: DataClassification
    ) -> Optional[pd.DataFrame]:
        """TDengine"""
        try:
            # 
            time_column = "ts" if "ts" in data.columns else "timestamp"
            if time_column not in data.columns:
                return data

            # 
            if "symbol" in data.columns:
                duplicates = data.duplicated(subset=[time_column, "symbol"])
            else:
                duplicates = data.duplicated(subset=[time_column])

            if duplicates.any():
                dup_count = duplicates.sum()
                logger.warning(
                    f"TDengine REJECT {dup_count} "
                )
                return pd.DataFrame()  # DataFrame

            # 
            return data

        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"TDengine REJECT: {e}")
            return data

            cursor = conn.cursor()

            #

            if success:
                conn.commit()
                self.monitoring_db.log_operation_result(operation_id, True, len(data))

                )

                self.monitoring_db.log_operation_result(
                    operation_id, False, 0, ""
                )

            return success

        except Exception as e:
            error_msg = f"PostgreSQL: {e}"
            self.monitoring_db.log_operation_result(operation_id, False, 0, error_msg)
            logger.error(error_msg)
            return False

            where_clause = " AND ".join([f"{col} = %s" for col in key_columns])

            # 
            update_columns = [col for col in data.columns if col not in key_columns]
            set_clause = ", ".join([f"{col} = %s" for col in update_columns])

            # 
            for _, row in data.iterrows():
                update_values = [row[col] for col in update_columns]
                key_values = [row[col] for col in key_columns]

                # SQL
                update_sql = f"""
                UPDATE {actual_table_name}
                SET {set_clause}
                WHERE {where_clause}
                """
                with engine.connect() as conn:
                    conn.execute(update_sql, list(update_values) + list(key_values))

            return True

        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"PostgreSQL: {e}")
            return False

    @abstractmethod
    def get_kline_data(
        self,
        symbol: str,
        start_time: datetime,
        end_time: datetime,
        interval: str = "1d",
    ) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """
        K

        Args:
            symbol: 
            start_time: 
            end_time: 
            interval: K
                     - : "1m", "5m", "15m", "30m", "60m"
                     - : "1d"

            DataFrame: K
                      - timestamp: 
                      - open: 
                      - high: 
                      - low: 
                      - close: 
                      - volume: 
                      - amount: 

        :
            timestamp           open    high    low     close   volume      amount
            2025-11-21 09:30   10.2    10.5    10.1    10.3    1250000     12800000
            2025-11-21 09:31   10.3    10.4    10.2    10.4    1180000     12200000
            ...

        :
            - (250): < 200ms
            - (1): < 300ms
            - (5): < 500ms

        Raises:
            DataSourceException: 
            ValueError: interval
        """
        pass

    @abstractmethod
    def get_intraday_chart(
        self, symbol: str, trade_date: Optional[date] = None
    ) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """

            symbol: 
            trade_date: None

            DataFrame:
